Hibernate: 
    select
        turn0_.id as id1_8_,
        turn0_.dice as dice2_8_,
        turn0_.round_id as round_id4_8_,
        turn0_.start_time as start_ti3_8_,
        turn0_.user_id as user_id5_8_ 
    from
        turn turn0_ 
    inner join
        user user1_ 
            on turn0_.user_id=user1_.id 
    inner join
        round round2_ 
            on turn0_.round_id=round2_.id 
    inner join
        game game3_ 
            on round2_.game_id=game3_.id 
    where
        user1_.nickname=? 
        and game3_.active=1 
    order by
        turn0_.round_id DESC

Hibernate: 
    select
        turn0_.id as id1_8_,
        turn0_.dice as dice2_8_,
        turn0_.round_id as round_id4_8_,
        turn0_.start_time as start_ti3_8_,
        turn0_.user_id as user_id5_8_ 
    from
        turn turn0_ 
    inner join
        user user1_ 
            on turn0_.user_id=user1_.id 
    inner join
        round round2_ 
            on turn0_.round_id=round2_.id 
    inner join
        game game3_ 
            on round2_.game_id=game3_.id 
    where
        user1_.nickname=? 
        and game3_.active=1 
    order by
        turn0_.round_id DESC
